<script>
(function(){
    Date.prototype.format = function(format) {
        var o = {
            "M+": this.getMonth() + 1,
            // month
            "d+": this.getDate(),
            // day
            "h+": this.getHours(),
            // hour
            "m+": this.getMinutes(),
            // minute
            "s+": this.getSeconds(),
            // second
            "q+": Math.floor((this.getMonth() + 3) / 3),
            // quarter
            "S": this.getMilliseconds()
            // millisecond
        };
        if (/(y+)/.test(format) || /(Y+)/.test(format)) {
            format = format.replace(RegExp.$1, (this.getFullYear() + "").substr(4 - RegExp.$1.length));
        }
        for (var k in o) {
            if (new RegExp("(" + k + ")").test(format)) {
                format = format.replace(RegExp.$1, RegExp.$1.length == 1 ? o[k] : ("00" + o[k]).substr(("" + o[k]).length));
            }
        }
        return format;
    };


    var counter = document.getElementById("mbox-entry-counter");
    var timeStamp = 1 * counter.getAttribute("data-timestamp");
    var icon = document.getElementById("mbox-entry-icon");
    var firstP = document.getElementById("welcome-first-p");

    var conterDown = function(){
        var now = new Date();
        counter.innerHTML = now.format("hh:mm");
        var hour = now.getHours();
        if ( hour < 9 && hour >= 5 ){
            icon.innerHTML = '<div class="icon-day"></div>';
            firstP.innerHTML = '现在是清晨';
        }
        else if ( hour < 13 && hour >= 9 ) {
            icon.innerHTML = '<div class="icon-day"></div>'
            firstP.innerHTML = '现在是上午';
        }
        else if ( hour < 17 && hour >= 13 ) {
            icon.innerHTML = '<div class="icon-day"></div>';
            firstP.innerHTML = '现在是午后';
        }
        else if ( hour < 20 && hour >= 17 ) {
            icon.innerHTML = '<div class="icon-night"></div>'
            firstP.innerHTML = '现在是傍晚';
        }
        else if ( hour < 4 || hour >= 20 ) {
            icon.innerHTML = '<div class="icon-night"></div>'
            firstP.innerHTML = '现在是夜晚';
        }

        timeStamp = timeStamp + 1;
    };
    setInterval(conterDown, 1000);

})();
</script>

				<script type="text/javascript">
					(function(){
						
						var random = function(t){ return Math.round(Math.random()*t) };
						var root = document.getElementById("js-random-focus");
						var randomOrder = function(root){
							var	elems = root.children,
								sectionOne = [], sectionTwo = [];
							for (var i = 0, l = elems.length; i < l; i++) {
								var cls = elems[i].className;
								if (cls == "js-random-first") {
									sectionOne.push(elems[i]);
								} else if (cls == "js-random-second") {
									sectionTwo.push(elems[i]);
								}
							}

							sectionTwo.length &&
							root.insertBefore(sectionTwo[random(sectionTwo.length - 1)], root.firstChild);
							sectionOne.length &&
							root.insertBefore(sectionOne[random(sectionOne.length - 1)], root.firstChild);

						};
						randomOrder(root);
						// 设置第一张图片的地址
						var firstFocus = root.getElementsByTagName("img")[0];
						if(window.narrowScreen){
							firstFocus.src = firstFocus.getAttribute("data-narrow");
						}else{
							firstFocus.src = firstFocus.getAttribute("data-wide");
						}

					})();

				</script>
